<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery(document).ready(function(e) {
    cookieChoices.showCookieConsentBar('<span class="cookie-choice-testo">Questo sito utilizza cookie, anche di terze parti, per inviarti pubblicit&agrave; e servizi in linea con le tue preferenze.<br>Se vuoi saperne di pi&ugrave; o negare il consenso a tutti o ad alcuni cookie <a href="http://www.casaeclima.com/st_99__CONTATTI-Privacy.html" class="cookie-choice-info">clicca qui</a>.<br>Chiudendo questo banner, scorrendo questa pagina o cliccando qualunque suo elemento acconsenti all\'uso dei cookie.</span>','<span class="btn btn-primary btn-xs cookie-choice-ok">OK</span>', '', '');
	jQuery(document).scroll(function(e) {
		if (jQuery('#cookieChoiceInfo').length > 0) {
			var expiryDate = new Date();
			expiryDate.setFullYear(expiryDate.getFullYear() + 1);
			document.cookie = 'displayCookieConsent' + '=y; expires=' + expiryDate.toGMTString();
			jQuery('#cookieChoiceInfo').remove();
		}
    });
	jQuery(document).mouseup(function (e) {
		var container = jQuery('#cookieChoiceInfo');
		if (container.length > 0) {
			if (!container.is(e.target) // if the target of the click isn't the container...
				&& container.has(e.target).length === 0) // ... nor a descendant of the container
			{
				var expiryDate = new Date();
				expiryDate.setFullYear(expiryDate.getFullYear() + 1);
				document.cookie = 'displayCookieConsent' + '=y; expires=' + expiryDate.toGMTString();
				container.remove();
			}
		}
	});	
	jQuery(window).unload(function(e) {
		if (jQuery('#cookieChoiceInfo').length > 0) {
			var expiryDate = new Date();
			expiryDate.setFullYear(expiryDate.getFullYear() + 1);
			document.cookie = 'displayCookieConsent' + '=y; expires=' + expiryDate.toGMTString();
			jQuery('#cookieChoiceInfo').remove();
		}
    });
	
});
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
var subCatHover = '';

jQuery.urlParam = function(name,url){
    var results = new RegExp('[\\?&amp;]' + name + '=([^&amp;#]*)').exec(url);
    return results[1] || 0;
}

/***********************
	DOM Ready Events
***********************/
jQuery(document).ready(function(){
	
	/***********************************
		Gestione Hover - Area Privata
	***********************************/
	jQuery('div.tool_areaprivata').hover(
		/* Mouse Over */
		function(){
			jQuery('div.tool_login').slideDown(200);
		},
		/* Mouse Out */
		function(){
			jQuery('div.tool_login').slideUp(200);
		}
	);  
	
	/*******************************
		Gestione Link Categorie
	*******************************/
	jQuery('a.link_menu_categoria').click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
		var idCategoria = '';
		if (jQuery(this).attr('id').length > 3) {
			idCategoria = jQuery(this).attr('id').substr(3);
		}
		if( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
		 	// some code..
		 	//verifico se ho un menu!
			if (jQuery('div.menuTOC_' + idCategoria).length == 0) {
				if (idCategoria != '') {
					var NomeCategoriaEsteso = jQuery(this).text().replace(/\s+/g,"-").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9.-]/g,"");
					jQuery(location).attr('href','/ct_' + encodeURIComponent(idCategoria) + '__' + encodeURIComponent(NomeCategoriaEsteso) + '.html');
				} else {
					jQuery(location).attr('href','/home_.html');
				}
			}
		} else {
			if (idCategoria != '') {
				var NomeCategoriaEsteso = jQuery(this).text().replace(/\s+/g,"-").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9.-]/g,"");
				jQuery(location).attr('href','/ct_' + encodeURIComponent(idCategoria) + '__' + encodeURIComponent(NomeCategoriaEsteso) + '.html');
			} else {
				jQuery(location).attr('href','/home_.html');
			}
		}
    });

	/***********************************
		Gestione Hover - Menu Selected
	***********************************/
	var timer;
	var delay_long = 500;
	var delay_short = 100;
	jQuery("div.menu span.sel:not(:contains('HOME')),div.menu a:not(:contains('HOME'))").hover(
		/* Mouse Over */
		function(){
			var myEl = jQuery(this);
			timer = setTimeout(function(){
				jQuery(this).addClass('hover');
				jQuery('div.divSubMenuCat').html(jQuery('div.menuTOC_' + myEl.attr('id').substr(3)).html());
				jQuery('div.divSubMenuCat').show();
			},delay_long);
		},
		/* Mouse Out */
		function(){
			clearTimeout(timer);
			setTimeout(function(){
				jQuery(this).removeClass('hover');
				if (!jQuery('div.divSubMenuCat').hasClass('hover')) {
					jQuery('div.divSubMenuCat').hide();
				}
			},delay_short);
		}
	);  
	
	//Gestione del MouseOver dal SottoMenu
	jQuery('div.divSubMenuCat').hover(
		function(){
			jQuery(this).addClass('hover');
		},
		function(){
			clearTimeout(timer);
			setTimeout(function(){
				jQuery('div.divSubMenuCat').removeClass('hover');
				var blocca = false;
				if(jQuery('div.menu span.sel').hasClass('hover')) {
					blocca = true;
				}
				jQuery('div.menu a').each(function(index, element) {
                    if ($(this).hasClass('hover')) {
						blocca = true;
						return false;
					}
                });
				if (!blocca) {
					jQuery('div.divSubMenuCat').hide();	
				}
			},100);
		}
	);

	/**************************
		HIde WowSlider sign
	**************************/
	jQuery.each(jQuery('body').find('a'),function(){
		if(jQuery(this).attr('href') == 'http://wowslider.com') {
			jQuery(this).hide();
		}
	});

	/*********************************
		Attivazione Riviste
	*********************************/
	jQuery('#totem-riviste').totemticker({
		row_height	:	'190px',
		next		:	'#totem-riviste-next',
		previous	:	'#totem-riviste-prev',
		stop		:	'#totem-riviste-stop',
		start		:	'#totem-riviste-start',
		mousestop	:	false
	});

	/*********************************
		Attivazione Scroller Bandi 
	*********************************/
	jQuery('#totem-bandi').totemticker({
		row_height	:	'120px',
		next		:	'#totem-bandi-next',
		previous	:	'#totem-bandi-prev',
		stop		:	'#totem-bandi-stop',
		start		:	'#totem-bandi-start',
		mousestop	:	false
	});
	jQuery('#totem-bandi-stop').click();
	setInterval(function(){
		jQuery('#totem-bandi-stop').click();
	},3000);

	/**********************************************
		Attivazione Scroller Bandi (sfasato 1 sec)
	**********************************************/
	setTimeout(function(){
		jQuery('#totem-eventi').totemticker({
			row_height: '120px',
			next: '#totem-eventi-next',
			previous: '#totem-eventi-prev',
			stop: '#totem-eventi-stop',
			start: '#totem-eventi-start',
			mousestop: true
		});
		jQuery('#totem-eventi-stop').click();
	},1000);

	/*************************************
		Attivazione Orologio Dinamico
	*************************************/
	setInterval(function(){impostaDataOra();}, 1000);

	/*********************
		Torna in cima 
	*********************/
	jQuery().UItoTop({ easingType: 'easeOutQuart' });

});
</script>

<script>
/**
* Function that tracks a click on an outbound link in Google Analytics.
* This function takes a valid URL string as an argument, and uses that URL string
* as the event label.
*/
var trackOutboundLink = function(url, new_window) {
  ga('send', 'event', 'outbound', 'click', url, {'hitCallback':
    function () {
      if (!new_window) {
        document.location = url;
		console.log('url tracciato - ga self - ' + url);
      }
    }
  });
  if (new_window){
  	console.log('url tracciato - ga blank - ' + url);
    window.open(url);
  }
}
jQuery(document).ready(function(){
  // [banner] set google analytics onclick link event on each link with class track
  jQuery('a.outga_track').each(function(index, element){
    element = jQuery(element);
    var link = element.attr('href');
	var idbanner = element.attr('data-banner');
    var new_window = element.attr('target') == '_blank' ? true : false;
    element.click(function(){
		updateClicks(idbanner);
      	trackOutboundLink(link, new_window);
      	return false;
    });
  });
  // [manchette] set google analytics onclick link event on each link with class track
  jQuery('a.outga_track_manchette').each(function(index, element){
    element = jQuery(element);
    var link = element.attr('href');
	var idmanchette = element.attr('data-manchette');
    var new_window = element.attr('target') == '_blank' ? true : false;
    element.click(function(){
		updateManchetteClicks(idmanchette,'sx_');
      	trackOutboundLink(link, new_window);
      	return false;
    });
  });
});
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
jQuery(document).ready(function(e) {
    jQuery('a.tool_op_esci').click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
		jConfirm('<span style="color:red; font-family:\'Anton\', sans-serif;">AVVISO</span>\n\nStai per uscire dal tuo account\n\nPremi <span style="font-weight:800">ESCI</span> per confermare','Casaeclima.com',function(r){
			if (r) {
				lockUI();
				location.href = '/logout.asp?SessionID=';
			}
		});
		jQuery('input#popup_ok').val('Esci');
		jQuery('input#popup_cancel').val('Annulla');
    });
	
	jQuery('a.tool_op_modifica').click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
		location.href = '/profilo.asp?SessionID=';
    });
	
	jQuery('form#formLogin').submit(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
		var parameters = jQuery(this).serialize();
		lockUI();
		jQuery.ajax({
			data: parameters,
			dataType: "JSON",
			type: "POST",
			url: "/json/controllo-login-json.asp",
			success: function(response) {
				if (response.esito == 'OK') {
					setTimeout(function(){
						location.href = response.urlaccesso;	
					},2000);
				} else {
					unLockUI();
					jAlert('<span style="color:red; font-family:\'Anton\', sans-serif;">!!! ACCESSO NEGATO !!!</span>\n\n' + response.motivo,'Casaeclima.com');
				}
			},
			error: function(msg) {
				unLockUI();
				jAlert('<span style="color:red; font-family:\'Anton\', sans-serif;">!!! ERRORE LOGIN !!!</span>\n\nSi &egrave; verificato un errore nel login.\n\nSi prega di riprovare pi&ugrave; tardi','Casaeclima.com');
			}
		});	
    });
	
	jQuery('form#formRicerca').submit(function(e) {
		//Controllo dati		
		if (TrimString(jQuery('input.tool_input_ricerca').val()) == '') {
			jAlert('<strong style="color:red;">!!! ATTENZIONE !!!</strong>\n\nimmettere il testo da cercare','CASA&amp;CLIMA.com',function(e){
				jQuery('input.tool_input_ricerca').focus();
			});
			return false;	
		}
        return true;
    });
	
	/**********************************
		Bind Bottone a Ricerca Sito
	**********************************/
	jQuery('input.btnCercaSito').click(function(e) {
        jQuery('form#formRicerca').submit();
    });
	
	/*******************************
		Bind Input Ricerca Sito
	*******************************/
	jQuery('input.tool_input_ricerca').keyup(function(e) {
        if (e.keyCode == 13) {
			jQuery('input.btnCercaSito').click();
		}
    });
});
</script>

			<img src="/thumbnail.asp?relpath=/public/casaeclima/1_a_b_aipe-saad-voci-capitolato.jpg&thumb=S&width=80&height=80" alt="/public/casaeclima/1_a_b_aipe-saad-voci-capitolato.jpg" width="50" style="margin-right:3px; float:left;" />			
			Sistemi costruttivi ad armatura diffusa (SAAD): da AIPE due voci di capitolato
            <br /><span style="font-weight:normal; font-family:'Dosis',sans-serif; font-size:14px; color:#000;">Valide per il computo metrico, prestazionale e descrittivo dell’opera dedicata alla parete ed al solaio</span>
            
    </a></div>
    
    <div class="riga" style="border-bottom:1px solid #c0c0c0;"><a href="/ar_31496__Outcome-Based-Service-nuovo-servizio-basato-cloud-gestione-edifici-.html" title="Outcome Based Service, un nuovo servizio basato su cloud per la gestione degli edifici ">
            
			<img src="/thumbnail.asp?relpath=/public/casaeclima/Immagini%20sito/2017/ACADEMY/OBS_CoverImage_%20low.jpg&thumb=S&width=80&height=80" alt="/public/casaeclima/Immagini%20sito/2017/ACADEMY/OBS_CoverImage_%20low.jpg" width="50" style="margin-right:3px; float:left;" />			
			Outcome Based Service, un nuovo servizio basato su cloud per la gestione degli edifici 
            <br /><span style="font-weight:normal; font-family:'Dosis',sans-serif; font-size:14px; color:#000;">La suite di servizi smart utilizza la connettività degli edifici per stabilire l’ordine di priorità delle attività di manutenzione, favorire le prestazioni ottimali delle strutture e ottenere ritorni economici</span>
            
    </a></div>
